posted:Posted June 4, 2024
msg:Five-star hotels in mainland China used to refer to software rather than hardware.
The whole hotel in Jingmin feels like it continues the style of a traditional five-star hotel.

It is extremely clean, the bed is good to sleep on, and the working atmosphere in the waiter room is excellent. When guests come over, each other will take the initiative to care and help - this sense of team is very strong, and each room has an exclusive room manager service. What are the characteristics of Fujian and Beijing? My feelings are still about "people".

In fact, the exclusive room manager service is not unique to Fujian and Beijing, such as Taipei Kagaya Hot Spring Hotel.
They are both called exclusive room managers but have completely different feelings. One is to show a smile at the beginning and then disappear completely; the other is to empathize with customers and think about how they can actually help to complete the needs raised by tenants. Manager Xiao Chen from Minjing belongs to the latter type. , thank you for her help and caring enthusiasm, coupled with the rare and sincere receptionist Li Cheng, who recognizes people but does not know their names...it made it a very good accommodation experience for me.

msg:Ten years have passed, and when I come here again, Jingmin's service is always online, always warming the heart of the guests, and making people remember it.
During the stay, a thoughtful gift was prepared for the baby, and a fruit platter was presented. Due to the delay of the plane, we arrived very late that night. The hotel has been waiting for the pick-up. The lobby manager kept asking about the situation and greeted us in the hotel lobby.

I brought my baby with me, and when I came back, I found that there was a lot more bottled water. It should be that the customer service staff saw that I needed more water to make milk, so I prepared a lot in advance, thank you very much.
Although the hotel hardware is old, the service is heart-warming and it is worth choosing.
